    SPRINT 74 - BUG FIX (Dashboard without Controller)
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    
    PROBLEM:
    Dashboard route loaded view directly without DashboardController, causing:
      ‚Ä¢ Undefined variable $stats (linha 48)
      ‚Ä¢ Attempt to read property on null (linha 48)
      ‚Ä¢ foreach() argument must be of type array (linha 48)
    
    ROOT CAUSE:
    File: public/index.php (linha 310-312)
    Route 'dashboard' called: require SRC_PATH . '/views/dashboard/index.php';
    Instead of instantiating DashboardController.
    
    SOLUTION (Surgical Fix):
    ```php
    // AFTER (linha 310-319):
    case 'dashboard':
        // SPRINT 74 FIX: Usar controller em vez de require direto
        require_once SRC_PATH . '/Controllers/DashboardController.php';
        $controller = new App\Controllers\DashboardController();
        $controller->index();
        break;
    ```
    
    RESULT:
    ‚úÖ Dashboard loads via controller
    ‚úÖ Variable $stats properly initialized
    ‚úÖ All 3 warnings eliminated
    ‚úÖ Cards display data correctly
